[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What happens  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `fuzz/xml.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invokes [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlCtxtParseDocument` on a crafted input.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. During parsing of the internal subset, `xmlParseInternalSubset` calls [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseEntityDecl`.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Inside `xmlParseEntityDecl`, entity values are parsed via [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseEntityValue`, which invokes `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue`.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Within `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue`, `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` attempts to copy [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe entity contents into a buffer.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. `__asan_memcpy` reads [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes beyond the end of a heap buffer that was only [0m[1;36m7[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes long, triggering the overflow.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The faulty read address [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x502000000b37[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lies immediately after a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte region[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated by `xmlFuzzMalloc` via `xmlStrndup`.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow is detected in a memcpy call at parser.[0m[1;92mc:777[0m[39m [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`xmlSBufAddEntitySecure`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The allocation originates in `xmlCreateEntity` → `xmlAddEntity` → [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlSAX2EntityDecl`, indicating entity data was duplicated but not sized for [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubsequent expansion.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The ASan shadow memory shows the right redzone being accessed, confirming a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer-too-small scenario.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • **xmlSBufAddEntitySecure** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.c around line [0m[1;36m777[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: buffer resizing and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemcpy logic.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • **xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue** and **xmlParseEntityValue** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: handling [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof parameter entity expansions and size accounting.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • **xmlParseEntityDecl** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: parsing flow for entity declarations, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincluding attribute values.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • **xmlCreateEntity** [0m[35m/[0m[39m **xmlAddEntity** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentities.c, SAX2.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: initial allocation[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof entity name/value strings.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • **xmlFuzzMalloc** and use of **xmlStrdup** in the fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzz/fuzz.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure allocations reflect maximum possible expansion.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Overall SBuf [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstring buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m management code in xmlstring.c/h: growth strategy,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mredzone margins, and memcpy bounds.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Entry point in **fuzz/xml.c** to understand how inputs are fed to the parser [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mthough the harness itself is not the root cause[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReviewing these components will provide a holistic view of how entity declarations [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare parsed, stored, and expanded—highlighting where buffer sizing and copying [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdiverge.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m378[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m379[0m[39m: * Returns the xmlChar * for the first occurrence or NULL.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m380[0m[39m: *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m381[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m382:c[0m[39monst xmlChar *[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m383[0m[39m:[0m[1;35mxmlStrcasestr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst xmlChar *str, const xmlChar *val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m384[0m[39m:    int n;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m385[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m386[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m387[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mval == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m388[0m[39m:    n = [0m[1;35mxmlStrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mval[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m389[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m390[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mn == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify the root cause[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The heap-buffer-overflow occurs because `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` only grows [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mits internal buffer on the very first addition [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhen `buf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Subsequent [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity expansions may require more space, but because the code never calls [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlSBufGrow` again, the call to `[0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->mem + buf->size, str, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` can [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceed the allocated capacity.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve existing logic and limits[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain the top‐of‐function check that ensures `buf->size + len` does not [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceed `buf->max` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe parser’s global “huge” or default text length limit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use the official `xmlSBufGrow` helper, which already implements a doubling [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrategy and a minimum allocation threshold [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m240[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, to resize the buffer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafely.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` in parser.c[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the special-case branch that only grows when `buf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` with a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconditional that checks whether the remaining capacity [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`buf->cap - buf->size`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mless than `len`. If so, invoke `[0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. The helper will compute an [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappropriate new capacity [0m[1;39m([0m[39mat least `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->size + len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m` and ≥[0m[1;36m240[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures that *every* call to add `len` bytes will first guarantee enough [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated space.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In pseudocode:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   static void [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlSBuf *buf, const xmlChar *str, unsigned [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlen[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->max - buf->size < len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m; return; [0m[1;39m}[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m OLD: if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len*[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m NEW:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap - buf->size < len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               return;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->mem + buf->size, str, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       buf->size += len;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` branch entirely and unify it under the one [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgrown‐when‐needed condition.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By mirroring the growth strategy in `xmlSBufAddString`, we ensure that every [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddition to the buffer is preceded by a capacity check and, if necessary, a safe [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreallocation.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This patch maintains the original resource‐limit logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`buf->max`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and does [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot weaken the parser’s protections against overly large entity expansions.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The use of `[0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` leverages existing doubling and [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mminimum‐size heuristics, avoiding arbitrary “magic” constants or manual [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalculations.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side effects & mitigation[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Memory overhead: growth will occur potentially more often for many small [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madditions, but `xmlSBufGrow` already minimizes reallocations by doubling the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequired size.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Performance: the additional capacity check [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`buf->cap - buf->size < len`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msingle integer comparison; the safety benefit far outweighs this trivial cost.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to harness, test code, or external libraries are needed; existing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests and fuzzing entry points will continue to function under the same API.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer harness targeting libxml2 triggered an AddressSanitizer [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow in parser.c’s function `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure`. The fuzzer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput exercises entity parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlParseInternalSubset` → `xmlParseEntityValue` → [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and over-reads [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes past a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte allocation. A [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch was applied in `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` to adjust the buffer-grow condition [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom checking `cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` to verifying `cap - size < len` and growing by `len` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than `len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m`. After rebuilding, the same ASAN overflow occurs at the same [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msite and with a similar stack trace, indicating the patch did not resolve the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer invocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`.[0m[35m/[0m[95mxml[0m[39m -[0m[33mrss_limit_mb[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m2560[0m[39m -[0m[33mtimeout[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m25[0m[39m -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m crashes inside AddressSanitizer.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow occurs in `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:777[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during a `memcpy` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes into a buffer that was only [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes long.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace shows nested calls: `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` → [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue` → `xmlParseEntityValue` → `xmlParseEntityDecl` → [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseInternalSubset` → `xmlParseDocument` → `xmlCtxtParseDocument` → fuzz [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ASAN reports the faulty read at address `[0m[1;36m0x502000000b37[0m[39m`, just beyond the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated region `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x502000000b30[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x502000000b37[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant Observations  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The buffer allocation originates from `xmlFuzzMalloc` → `xmlStrdup` → [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlCreateEntity` → `xmlAddEntity` → `xmlSAX2EntityDecl`.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The buggy call copies entity data without confirming the buffer can accommodate [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit.  [0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow is reproducible under libFuzzer with both seeds shown.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `parser.c`, lines around `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` were modified:  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```diff[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  -    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  -        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Ensure that the buffer is double the necessary size[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  -        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m This ensures no buffer overflow is possible[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  -        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  +    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap - buf->size < len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  +        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The old logic grew the buffer only if `cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`, doubling the requested length; [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe new logic grows whenever the remaining capacity is less than `len`, but only by[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`len` instead of `[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m*len`.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Result  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- After rebuilding and rerunning the same fuzzing command, AddressSanitizer reports[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same heap-buffer-overflow at `parser.[0m[1;92mc:775[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39madjusted line numbers after [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace and allocation site remain effectively unchanged, indicating that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe new growth condition did not prevent the overflow.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The implementation of `xmlSBufGrow`: verify that it increases `cap` by at least [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`len + buffer margin` and updates `size` appropriately.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The invariants around `buf->size` and `buf->cap` in [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlSBufAddEntitySecure`—ensure the logic accounts for all code paths that append [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m892[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mxmlSBufReportError[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ctxt, errMsg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m893[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m894[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->mem[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m895[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m896[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m897[0m[39m:static int[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m898[0m[39m:[0m[1;35mxmlUTF8MultibyteLen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlParserCtxtPtr ctxt, const xmlChar *str,[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m899[0m[39m:                    const char *errMsg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m900[0m[39m:    int c = str[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:761[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m779[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m761[0m[39m:static void[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m762[0m[39m:[0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlSBuf *buf, const xmlChar *str, unsigned len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m763[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->max - buf->size < len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m764[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->code == XML_ERR_OK[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m765[0m[39m:            buf->code = XML_ERR_RESOURCE_LIMIT;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m766[0m[39m:        return;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m767[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m768[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m769[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m770[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Ensure that the buffer is double the necessary size[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m771[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m This ensures no buffer overflow is possible[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m772[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m773[0m[39m:            return;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m774[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m775[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m776[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m777[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->mem + buf->size, str, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m778[0m[39m:    buf->size += len;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m779[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root-Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The AddressSanitizer crash is happening in xmlSBufAddEntitySecure’s memcpy, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreading more bytes from the source string than were allocated. In the [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDTD‐entity‐expansion code [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, there is one branch that [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoes:  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->name, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Here, `ent->length` is the length of the entity’s **content**, but the code is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassing `ent->name` as the source. As a result, memcpy reads `ent->length` bytes [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the `name` buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39monly allocated to hold the name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, overflowing the source [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Additionally, xmlSBufAddEntitySecure only ever grows its internal buffer on the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfirst write [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`buf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so subsequent large or repeated appends can overflow[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe destination buffer as well.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. High-Level Fix Outline  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. **Correct the arguments** in the expansion site: when inserting a parameter [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity’s data, pass the **content** pointer and the content length, not the name [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer and content length.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. **Harden xmlSBufAddEntitySecure** so that it grows its buffer on *every* [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappend when needed, just like the other xmlSBufAdd* helpers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlSBufAddEntity` and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlSBufAddString`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, thereby preventing any write‐side overflows in deep or large [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnestings.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. In parser.c, locate the problematic branch in `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39maround line ~[0m[1;36m4003[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m old buggy code[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, str - chunk[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->name, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Replace it with:  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m grow for the literal chunk[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr - chunk[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m append the parameter entity’s content [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot its name[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->content, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This ensures memcpy’s source pointer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ent->content`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and byte count [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`ent->length`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m match, preventing any source‐side overread.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. In parser.c, find the definition of `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m761[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m779[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Replace the one‐time‐only growth logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m …`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mper‐append capacity check that mirrors `xmlSBufAddEntity`:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```diff[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     static void[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlSBuf *buf, const xmlChar *str, unsigned len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m enforce the parser’s max‐length invariant[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->max - buf->size < len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->code == XML_ERR_OK[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 buf->code = XML_ERR_RESOURCE_LIMIT;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m [0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-            [0m[35m/[0m[39m* old logic: only grow once, doubling requested size *[0m[35m/[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-                return;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* grow as needed on every append *[0m[35m/[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap - buf->size < len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+                return;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m [0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->mem + buf->size, str, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         buf->size += len;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This patch prevents any write‐side overflows by ensuring the buffer’s remaining [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcapacity always meets the requested `len`.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification & Impact  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – **Correct Source Read**: By passing `ent->content` instead of `ent->name`, we [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminate the heap‐buffer‐overflow on the *source* side of memcpy.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – **Prevent Destination Overflows**: The revised growth check makes sure the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minternal buffer is grown whenever necessary, not just on the first use, aligning [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith the behavior of `xmlSBufAddEntity`.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – **Preserve Core Logic**: We still enforce `buf->max` to prevent “billion [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlaughs”–style amplification and continue to propagate the same error codes [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`XML_ERR_RESOURCE_LIMIT`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. No other code paths, harness logic, or tests are [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodified.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – **Side Effects**:  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Slightly more frequent buffer‐growth calls in pathological DTDs—but that is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready tolerated by other xmlSBufAdd* helpers.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • No change to XML semantics; parameter entity content expansion remains [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentical.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – **Consistency**: This matches the pattern already used by `xmlSBufAddEntity` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `xmlSBufAddString`, making the API uniform and easier to maintain.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Verification  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Rebuild libxml2 and re-run the libFuzzer harness. The previous ASAN crash in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` should no longer occur.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Run the full internal test suite to confirm no regressions in entity parsing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor other DTD behavior.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
